    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.status = @__status_Value_0
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

FROM (
    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted)
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted)
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id

LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (

    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

FROM (
    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted)
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.admission_date, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.discharge_date, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.leave_granted, i0.patient_age, i0.patient_gender, i0.patient_profession, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.request_id = @__requestId_0
ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC

FROM (
    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted)
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

FROM (
    SELECT i.id, i.admission_date, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.discharge_date, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.leave_granted, i.patient_age, i.patient_gender, i.patient_profession, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i
    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.status = @__status_Value_0
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.admission_date, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.discharge_date, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.leave_granted, i1.patient_age, i1.patient_gender, i1.patient_profession, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC
